Regulation S-T Rule&nbsp;101 (b)(7): </font><font size="2" face="Wingdings" style="font-size:10.0pt;">o</font></p>

paper of a Form&nbsp;6-K if submitted to furnish a report or other document
that the registrant foreign private issuer must furnish and make public under
the laws of the jurisdiction in which the registrant is incorporated, domiciled
or legally organized (the registrant&#146;s &#147;home country&#148;), or under the rules&nbsp;of
the home country exchange on which the registrant&#146;s securities are traded, as
long as the report or other document is not a press release, is not required to
be and has not been distributed to the registrant&#146;s security holders, and, if
discussing a material event, has already been the subject of a Form&nbsp;6-K
submission or other Commission filing on EDGAR.</font></p>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and Corporate Secretary</font></p>
  </td>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;1</font></b></p>

<div align="center">

  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.76%;">

  <td width="43%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:43.24%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(All
amounts expressed in U.S. dollars unless otherwise noted)</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AGNICO-EAGLE REPORTS Q3 2010 RESULTS;<br>
RECORD QUARTERLY NET INCOME;</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">RECORD QUARTERLY GOLD PRODUCTION AT MEADOWBANK,
GOLDEX, KITTILA AND PINOS ALTOS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Toronto
(October&nbsp;27, 2010) &#151; Agnico-Eagle Mines Limited</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(&#147;Agnico-Eagle&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) today reported a record
quarterly net income of $121.5 million, or $0.73 per share, for the third quarter
of 2010.&#160; This result includes a non-cash
foreign currency translation loss of $17.7 million, or $0.11 per share.&#160; The result also includes non-cash stock-based
compensation expense of $8.4 million, or $0.05 per share.&#160; More than offsetting these items, was a gain
on the acquisition of Comaplex Minerals&#146; Meliadine property of $57.5 million
(net of acquisition costs), or $0.34 per share.&#160;
Additionally, the Company recorded a gain on the sale of
available-for-sale securities and a property disposition totaling $16.6
million, or $0.10 per share and a one-time tax restructuring loss of $5.6
million, or $0.03 per share.&#160; In the
third quarter of 2009, the Company reported a net loss of $17.0 million, or
$0.11 per share.&#160; A 140% increase in gold
production and a 233% increase in gross mine profit(1)&nbsp;over the third
quarter of 2009 contributed to the record financial and operating quarter.</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)&nbsp; Gross mine profit is calculated as total revenues from all
metals, by mine, minus total production costs, by mine.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2010 cash provided by
operating activities was $156.8 million ($170.9 million before changes in
non-cash components of working capital), up from cash used in operating
activities of $13.8 million in the third quarter of 2009 ($38.6 million before
changes in non-cash components of working capital).&#160; This significant increase was largely due to
the previously mentioned increase in gold production and substantially higher
prices for gold, zinc, silver and copper.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2010 highlights include:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Record Gold Production,</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  <b>Record</b>  <b>Revenue and Record Net Earnings </b>&#151; quarterly gold production
of 285,178 ounces resulted in revenue of $398.5 million and net earnings of
$121.5 million</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Record Cash Flows </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151; excluding non-cash changes in working capital, $170.9
million versus the prior quarter&#146;s record of $138.9 million</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Record quarterly gold recovery at Kittila </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151; with the 81% recovery in the mill at Kittila, the design
rate of 83% is on target for year end 2010</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Creston Mascota at Pinos Altos about to
Start-Up &#151; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">crushing
plant has been commissioned and loading of leach pads scheduled to begin in
fourth quarter</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\bvanga\10-20133-1\task4330503\20133-1-ka-01.htm',USER='bvanga',CD='Oct 29 00:58 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The transformational phase at
Agnico-Eagle is complete and has resulted in record earnings and cash flows per
share.&#160; The next phase, one of
optimization and expansion of our newly built mines, is underway.&#160; As a result, we expect gold production and
cash flows to continue to grow&#148; said Sean Boyd, Vice-Chairman and Chief
Executive Officer.&#160; &#147;We look forward to
reinvesting part of these growing cash flows to expand output, grow gold
reserves and increase our longstanding dividend&#148; added Mr.&nbsp;Boyd.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable gold production(2)&nbsp;in
the third quarter of 2010 was a record 285,179 ounces at total cash costs per
ounce(3)&nbsp;of $441.&#160; This compares with
payable gold production of 118,763 ounces at total cash costs per ounce of $436
in the third quarter of 2009.</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)&nbsp; Payable production of a
mineral means the quantity of mineral produced during a period contained in
products that are sold by the Company, whether such products are shipped during
the period or held as inventory at the end of the period.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)&nbsp; Total cash costs per ounce
is a non-GAAP measure.&#160; For
reconciliation of this measure to production costs, as reported in the
financial statements, see Note 1 to the financial statements at the end of this
press release.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The total cash costs were
essentially unchanged versus the prior year&#146;s quarter.&#160; Significant byproduct revenues at LaRonde
resulted in total cash costs of <i>negative</i> $298
per ounce at that mine.&#160; Also
contributing strongly was Goldex with record quarterly gold production and good
cost control ($288/oz).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Higher than anticipated total cash
costs remain at Meadowbank ($677/oz) as this new mine moves through start-up
and commissioning.&#160; Additionally, total
cash costs per ounce at Pinos Altos were $690 in the third quarter of 2010
versus $415 in the second quarter of 2010.&#160;
This increase at Pinos Altos is mainly due to the first ore from the
underground operation (relatively high start-up costs), the one-time lump-sum
payment of an annual bonus to workers (will be accrued going forward) and, most
significantly, due to the stockpile inventory adjustments (wrote down a
low-grade stockpile).&#160; While the industry
has seen higher costs for major inputs such as reagents (specifically cyanide)
and labour, total cash costs per ounce at both of these mines are expected to
decline as gold production increases.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the first nine months of 2010,
payable gold production was a record 731,138 ounces at total cash costs per
ounce of $459.&#160; This compares with
payable gold production of 329,628 ounces at total cash costs per ounce of $368
in the first nine months of 2009.&nbsp; The increase in gold production is due
to the impact of two new gold mines commencing operations in the past
year.&#160; The increase in total cash costs
per ounce in the first nine months of 2010 is mainly due to the higher than
expected total cash costs per ounce at Meadowbank ($682/oz) and Pinos Altos ($527),
neither of which were operating in the first nine months of 2009.</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the full year 2010, gold
production is still expected to be in line with previous guidance of between
1.0 and 1.1 million ounces.&#160; The Company&#146;s
forecast for its full year total cash cost per ounce remains unchanged from the
second quarter 2010 guidance of approximately $425 to $450.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2<a name="PB_2_004854_5335"></a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash Position
Remains Strong</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cash and cash equivalents were
essentially unchanged at $148.1 million on September&nbsp;30, 2010 from the June&nbsp;30,
2010 balance of $152.8 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Capital expenditures in the third
quarter of 2010 were $167.1 million, including $74.1 million at Meadowbank,
$28.2 million at Pinos Altos, $25.5 million at LaRonde, $21.1 million at
Kittila, $7.1 million at Lapa, $6.0 million at Goldex and $3.6 million at
Meliadine. For 2010, capital expenditures are estimated to remain unchanged at
approximately $506 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With its cash balances, anticipated
cash flows and available bank lines, Agnico-Eagle remains fully funded for the
development and exploration of its current pipeline of gold projects in Canada,
Finland, Mexico and the USA.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Available bank lines as of September&nbsp;30,
2010 were approximately $1.1 billion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">LaRonde Mine &#151; Steady State Mine Continues
Strong Performance</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The LaRonde mill processed an
average of 6,872 tonnes per day (&#147;tpd&#148;) of ore in the third quarter of 2010,
compared with an average of 6,509 tpd in the corresponding period of 2009.&#160; The increase in throughput in 2010 reflects
an extended maintenance shutdown in the 2009 period which did not recur in
2010.&#160; Overall, LaRonde has been
operating at a steady state of approximately 7,000 tpd for approximately seven
years, since its most recent expansion in 2003.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3<a name="PB_3_004942_5796"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne(4)&nbsp;were
C$74 in the third quarter of 2010, essentially unchanged when compared to C$73
in the third quarter of 2009.</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)&nbsp; Minesite costs per tonne
is a non-GAAP measure.&#160; For
reconciliation of this measure to production costs, as reported in the
financial statements, see Note 1 to the financial statements at the end of this
news release.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the first nine months of 2010,
minesite costs per tonne were slightly below budget at C$74.&#160; For the first nine months of 2009, the
minesite costs per tonne were C$72.&#160; The
increase is largely due to general cost inflation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net of byproduct credits, LaRonde&#146;s
total cash costs per ounce were <i>negative</i> $298
in the third quarter of 2010 on production of 37,832 ounces of gold.&#160; During the third quarter of 2009, total cash
costs per ounce were $60 on production of 47,726 ounces of gold.&#160; The decrease in total cash costs is largely
due to higher byproduct revenues, partly offset by the lower gold
production.&#160; The lower production was
mainly due to an expected decrease in gold grade for ore mined in 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the first nine months of 2010,
LaRonde&#146;s total cash costs per ounce were $69 on gold production of 124,401
ounces, as compared to the first nine months of 2009, when the total cash costs
per ounce were $148<i>  </i>on<i>  </i>production of 157,098 ounces of gold.&#160; The lower total cash costs were largely due
to higher byproduct metals revenues, as noted above.&#160; Similarly, the lower production is mainly due
to the lower gold grade (approximately 23% lower) mined in 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Commencing in late 2011, when the
Company expects to begin mining ore from the LaRonde Extension, LaRonde is
expected to begin producing more gold, averaging 324,000 ounces of gold per
year from 2014 through 2023, reflecting the higher gold grades at depth.&#160; The development of the LaRonde Extension
remains on time and on budget.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Goldex &#151; Record Production and Good Cost
Control</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Goldex mill processed an average
of 7,893 tpd in the third quarter of 2010, continuing to exceed the 2010 mine
plan of approximately 6,900 tpd.&#160; During
the third quarter of 2009, the plant processed 7,342 tpd.&#160; Goldex is now operating close to its expanded
steady-state rate of 8,000 tpd.&#160; This
expansion is essentially complete, ahead of schedule.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Goldex
were approximately C$21 in the third quarter of 2010, in line with the C$21 per
tonne achieved in the third quarter of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable gold production in the third
quarter of 2010 was 50,672 ounces at total cash costs per ounce of $288.&#160; This compares favourably to the third quarter
of 2009 when gold production was 31,169 ounces at total cash costs per ounce of
$428.&#160; The higher ounce output is largely
due to the higher throughput and the resumption of mining from the higher grade
central pillar, when compared to 2009 (grade up 45% over the comparable
period).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the nine months ended September&nbsp;30,
2010, total cash costs at Goldex were $325 per ounce on gold production of
141,275 ounces.&#160; Total cash costs per
ounce during the comparable nine month period in 2009 were $371 on gold
production of 102,774 ounces.&#160; The
improvement in production and costs continues to reflect optimization of
throughput and the resumption of mining in the higher grade central pillar.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Life of mine average annual gold
production is expected to be approximately 168,000 ounces per year through
2017.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The final production blast for the
current orebody is scheduled for late 2010 (to be followed by approximately
seven years of extraction).&#160; As a result,
the focus has shifted to exploration and potentially extending the mine life by
adding nearby zones, such as the &#147;M&#148;, &#147;D&#148;, &#147;E&#148; and &#147;S&#148; zones, into the mine
plan.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development is already underway on
the &#147;M&#148; zone, while studies on the other zones are expected to be completed in
2011.&#160; First production from the &#147;M&#148; zone
is expected to be in 2013.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Lapa &#151;
Strong Tonnage and Cost Performance Continue</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Lapa milling circuit, located at LaRonde, processed an average of 1,573 tpd in
the third quarter of 2010, compared to 1,179 tpd in the third quarter of
2009.&#160; This increase reflects the
continued optimization efforts at the mine and mill where both facets at Lapa
continue to operate above budgeted levels.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite
costs per tonne were below budget at C$105 in the third quarter of 2010, and
well below the C$142 incurred in the third quarter of 2009.&#160; This reduction in cost reflects the
optimization and efficiencies which have been realized since the May&nbsp;2009
start-up.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable
production in the third quarter of 2010 was 27,688 ounces of gold at total cash
costs per ounce of $509. This compares to 18,409 ounces of gold at total cash
costs per ounce of $784 during the third quarter of 2009.&#160; The higher production and lower costs reflect
the optimization since start-up.&#160;
Specifically, mine personnel have been successful in increasing the
throughput to offset the dilution underground.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the nine month period ending September&nbsp;30,
2010, total cash costs at Lapa were $517 per ounce on gold production of 88,168
ounces.&#160; This compares with gold
production of 30,013 ounces at total cash costs of $832 in the partial first
nine months of 2009.&#160; This production
increase and unit cost decrease is largely due to improved throughput,
optimization and its associated efficiencies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Life of mine production is expected
to be approximately 116,000 ounces of gold through 2015.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kittila &#151; Mill Optimization in Final Stages</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Kittila mill processed an
average of 3,067 tpd in the third quarter of 2010, compared to 1,958 tpd in the
third quarter of 2009.&#160; The design
throughput rate at Kittila is 3,000 tpd.&#160;
The higher rate in 2010 is due to continued optimization efforts since
the January&nbsp;2009 start-up.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Gold recoveries in the third quarter
of 2010 averaged a record high of approximately 81%, up significantly from the
68% achieved in the second quarter of 2010 and the 64% realized </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">in the third quarter of 2009.&#160; The higher recoveries were largely due to a
series of process changes that were implemented in the second and third
quarters of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The improvement in the process was
largely due to the control and reduction of the chloride compound levels in the
autoclave.&#160; The design rate of 83% mill
recovery is expected to be achieved on a steady state basis by the end of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Kittila
were approximately &#128;58 in the third quarter of 2010, an improvement from the
&#128;78 achieved in the third quarter of 2009.&#160;
The decrease in minesite costs is largely due to the higher throughput.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2010 gold production
at Kittila was a record 40,344 ounces at total cash costs per ounce of $519,
compared to 18,284 ounces at cash costs per ounce of $1,080 in the third
quarter of 2009.&#160; This improvement is
largely due to higher mill recoveries and improved throughput, facilitated by
the ongoing, consistent, performance of the mine.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the nine month period ending September&nbsp;30,
2010, total cash costs at Kittila were $603 per ounce on gold production of
96,484 ounces.&#160; This compares with gold
production of 36,568 ounces at total cash costs of $1,041 in the partial first
nine months of 2009.&#160; This improvement is
largely due to higher mill recoveries and improved throughput since start-up.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Underground production is now
underway at Kittila and ground conditions are encouraging.&#160; Total underground production is expected to account
for approximately 10% of Kittila&#146;s 2010 production.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Life of mine average gold production
is expected to be approximately 150,000 ounces per year through 2032.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A
study is underway examining the possibility of increasing the production rate
at Kittila reflecting the continued growth of the reserve base.&#160; Assuming the successful optimization of the
mill recoveries, and further drilling at depth and to the north of the main
Suuri deposit, it is anticipated that the expansion study will be completed by
the middle of 2011.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pinos Altos &#151; Achieving Design Throughput.&#160; Additional Filter Capacity Installed</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle
is proud to announce that the Pinos Altos mine was the winner of Mexico&#146;s 2009 &#147;Casco
de Plata&#148; (&#147;Silver Hard Hat&#148;) safety award recognizing the mine as the number
one safety performer nationally during 2009 in the large open pit mine
category.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Pinos Altos mill processed an average of 3,863 tpd in the third quarter of
2010, representing an improvement over the prior quarter (3,575 tpd) as the
ramp up to the design rate of 4,000 tpd continues. No comparable period exists
in 2009 as the mine achieved commercial production in November.&#160;&#160; Commissioning of a fourth tailings filter
commenced in the last week of September&nbsp;and a fifth tailings filter will
be commissioned in November, which is expected to eliminate tailings filtration
as a bottleneck in the mill.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne were $50 in
the third quarter of 2010, compared to $31 in the prior quarter.&#160; The increase in minesite costs was largely
due to a stockpile adjustment, the payment of a special bonus to workers and
the start-up of the underground mining operation, as previously </font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">mentioned.&#160; Without the impact of the stockpile adjustment,
the minesite costs per tonne would have been $40 in the third quarter of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite
costs per tonne were $39 for the first nine months of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Some
temporary production delays have been experienced in the new underground mine
as several historic artisanal openings had to be emptied and backfilled.&#160; These artisanal openings only impact the
upper part of the Santo Nino underground orebody.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Lateral
development and stope preparation is ahead of schedule.&#160; Ground conditions in the mined stopes have
been better than expected, which should allow rapid increases in underground
production in the coming months along with lower unit costs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable
production from the mill and heap leach operations in the third quarter of 2010
was a record 35,248 ounces of gold at total cash costs per ounce of $690.&#160; This compares with the second quarter of
2010, which had payable gold production of 29,665 ounces at total cash costs
per ounce of $415.&#160; The increase in total
cash costs from the second quarter of 2010 is largely due to the previously
discussed factors.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the first nine months of 2010, payable gold production was 91,141 ounces at
total cash costs of $527 per ounce.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Life of mine average gold production
is expected to be approximately 170,000 ounces per year through 2028, including
production from Creston Mascota.&#160; Over
this period, annual silver production is expected to average 2.5 million
ounces.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Civil
works and mechanical construction are close to completion at the nearby Creston
Mascota project.&#160; First ore is expected
to be placed on the leach pads during the fourth quarter of 2010.&#160; This stand-alone mine is expected to achieve
commercial production in the second quarter of 2011.&#160; Production of approximately 50,000 ounces of
gold per year is expected over five years at this project.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank
&#151; Tonnage Ramp-Up Continues</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the third quarter of 2010,
the Meadowbank mill processed an average of 6,918 tpd.&#160; Throughput in the prior quarter, its first
full quarter of operation, totaled 6,262 tpd.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In spite of this improvement in
throughput, unit costs have been negatively impacted by crushing issues, as
discussed last quarter.&#160; To attempt to
resolve these issues, and achieve the design rate of 8,500 tpd on a consistent
basis, the Company will install a permanent secondary crushing unit at the
front end of the circuit.&#160; This solution
was successfully adopted at Goldex during its commissioning phase.&#160; This secondary crusher should be installed
and operational early in the third quarter of 2011.&#160; In the meantime, two portable crushing units
are being used.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne were higher
than planned at C$103 in the third quarter of 2010.&#160; This compares with the second quarter of 2010
when minesite costs per tonne were C$94.&#160;
The higher costs are due to higher drilling and hauling costs as low
availability of equipment led to increased use of contractors.&#160; Also impacting costs were some major
equipment repairs, pre-crushing at the mill and higher logistics expenses.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7<a name="PB_7_005137_141"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='7',FILE='C:\JMS\bvanga\10-20133-1\task4330503\20133-1-ka-01.htm',USER='bvanga',CD='Oct 29 00:58 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It is expected that minesite costs
per tonne will begin to drop in the fourth quarter of 2010, as larger, more
efficient haul trucks and shovels are commissioned.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable production during the third
quarter of 2010 was 93,395 ounces of gold, at total cash costs per ounce of
$677.&#160; This compares with payable
production of 77,676 ounces at total cash costs per ounce of $663 in the prior
quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Year to date, gold production is
189,669 ounces at total cash costs of $682 per ounce.&#160; These costs are expected to begin to decline
in the fourth quarter as operational improvements are realized and the larger
equipment is utilized.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Life of mine average annual gold
production is expected to be approximately 350,000 ounces through 2019.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A
study examining the possibility of increasing the production rate at Meadowbank
is partially complete.&#160; The study was
scheduled to be completed in 2010, however, due to ongoing optimization
efforts, the study is being delayed until the mine reaches steady state and further
underground drilling is completed.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meliadine Acquisition Complete, Exploration
Program Begins</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On July&nbsp;6, 2010, Agnico-Eagle
completed the acquisition of 100% of the Meliadine gold property (through the
acquisition of Comaplex Minerals Corp.), located approximately 300 kilometres
southeast of the Company&#146;s Meadowbank mine.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Through early 2013, it is
anticipated that approximately $62 million will be spent on drilling an
anticipated 200,000 metres with the main focus being on converting the resource
at the high grade Tiriganiaq deposit to reserves.&#160; An underground bulk sample will also be
completed along with a feasibility study, permitting and permanent all-weather
road construction.&#160; The total
expenditures, including drilling, over this period are expected to be
approximately $130 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Initial results from this drilling
program, and those for some of Agnico-Eagle&#146;s other exploration programs,
including Kittila, will be presented in an exploration update planned for December&nbsp;2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Agnico-Eagle</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle is a long established,
Canadian headquartered, gold producer with operations located in Canada,
Finland and Mexico, and exploration and development activities in Canada,
Finland, Mexico and the United States.&#160;
Agnico-Eagle&#146;s LaRonde mine is Canada&#146;s largest operating gold mine in
terms of reserves.&#160; The Company has full
exposure to higher gold prices consistent with its policy of no forward gold
sales.&#160; It has paid a cash dividend for
28 consecutive years.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8<a name="PB_8_005207_7608"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Note 1</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Gross mine profit is calculated as total revenues from all metals, by
mine, minus total production costs, by mine.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Note 2</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Meadowbank achieved commercial production as of March&nbsp;1,
2010.&#160; Payable production includes
commercial production of 188,585 ounces since March&nbsp;1, 2010 and
non-commercial production of 1,084 ounces.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Note 3</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total cash costs per ounce of gold is calculated net of silver, copper,
zinc and other byproduct credits. The weighted average total cash cost per
ounce is based on commercial production ounces.&#160;
Total cash costs per ounce is a non-GAAP measure.&#160; For a reconciliation to production costs, see
Note 1 to the financial statements.&#160; See
also &#147;Note Regarding Certain Measures of Performance&#148;.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Note 4</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Certain measures have been reclassified in prior periods to conform to
the current periods&#146; presentation.&#160; The
changes are immaterial in nature.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AGNICO-EAGLE
MINES LIMITED</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CONSOLIDATED
BALANCE SHEETS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(thousands
of United States dollars, US GAAP basis)</font></b></p>

  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;border:none;border-bottom:double windowtext 2.25pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.3%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">$</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="12%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;border-bottom:double windowtext 2.25pt;border-left:none;border-right:none;border-top:double windowtext 2.25pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:12.22%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">98</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;border:none;border-bottom:double windowtext 2.25pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.3%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">$</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="12%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;border-bottom:double windowtext 2.25pt;border-left:none;border-right:none;border-top:double windowtext 2.25pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:12.22%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.1%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.45pt;text-indent:-37.45pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Under the
Company&#146;s revenue recognition policy, revenue is recognized on concentrates
when legal title passes. Since total cash costs are calculated on a production
basis, this inventory adjustment reflects the sales margin on the portion of
concentrate production for which revenue has not been recognized in
the&nbsp;period.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.45pt;text-indent:-37.45pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total cash
costs per ounce is not a recognized measure under US GAAP and this data may not
be comparable to data presented by other gold producers. The Company believes
that this generally accepted industry measure is a realistic indication of
operating performance and is useful in allowing year over year comparisons. As
illustrated in the table above, this measure is calculated by adjusting
production costs as shown in the Consolidated Statements of Income and
Comprehensive Income for net byproduct revenues, royalties, inventory
adjustments and asset retirement provisions. This measure is intended to
provide investors with information about the cash generating capabilities of
the Company&#146;s mining operations. Management uses this measure to monitor the
performance of the Company&#146;s mining operations. Since market prices for gold
are quoted on a per ounce basis, using this per ounce measure allows management
to assess the mine&#146;s cash generating capabilities at various gold prices.
Management is aware that this per ounce measure of performance can be impacted
by fluctuations in byproduct metal prices and exchange rates. Management
compensates for the limitation inherent with this measure by using it in
conjunction with the minesite costs per tonne measure (discussed below) as well
as other data prepared in accordance with US GAAP. Management also performs
sensitivity analyses in order to quantify the effects of fluctuating metal
prices and exchange&nbsp;rates.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">20<a name="PB_20_014306_5250"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='20',FILE='C:\JMS\bvanga\10-20133-1\task4330775\20133-1-ka-05.htm',USER='bvanga',CD='Oct 29 02:15 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.45pt;text-indent:-37.45pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This inventory
adjustment reflects production costs associated with unsold concentrates.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.45pt;text-indent:-37.45pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs
per tonne is not a recognized measure under US GAAP and this data may not be
comparable to data presented by other gold producers. As illustrated in the
table above, this measure is calculated by adjusting production costs as shown
in the Consolidated Statements of Income and Comprehensive Income for inventory
and asset retirement provisions and then dividing by tonnes processed through
the mill. Since total cash costs data can be affected by fluctuations in byproduct
metal prices and exchange rates, management believes minesite costs per tonne
provides additional information regarding the performance of mining operations
and allows management to monitor operating costs on a more consistent basis as
the per tonne measure eliminates the cost variability associated with varying
production levels. Management also uses this measure to determine the economic
viability of mining blocks. As each mining block is evaluated based on the net
realizable value of each tonne mined, in order to be economically viable the
estimated revenue on a per tonne basis must be in excess of the minesite costs
per tonne. Management is aware that this per tonne measure is impacted by
fluctuations in production levels and thus uses this evaluation tool in
conjunction with production costs prepared in accordance with US GAAP. This
measure supplements production cost information prepared in accordance with US
GAAP and allows investors to distinguish between changes in production costs
resulting from changes in production versus changes in operating performance.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Note Regarding
Certain Measures of Performance</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press
release presents measures including &#147;total cash costs per ounce&#148; and &#147;minesite
costs per tonne&#148; that are not recognized measures under US GAAP. This data may
not be comparable to data presented by other gold producers. The Company
believes that these generally accepted industry measures are realistic
indicators of operating performance and useful for year-over-year comparisons.
However, both of these non-GAAP measures should be considered together with
other data prepared in accordance with US GAAP, these measures, taken by
themselves, are not necessarily indicative of operating costs or cash flow
measures prepared in accordance with US GAAP. A reconciliation of the Company&#146;s
total cash cost per ounce and minesite cost per tonne to the most comparable
financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with US GAAP for the
Company&#146;s historical results of operations is set out in Note 1 to the
financial statements of the Company for the period ended September&nbsp;30,
2010 contained herein.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
contents of this press release have been prepared under the supervision of, and
reviewed by, Marc Legault P.Eng., Vice-President Project Development and a &#147;Qualified
Person&#148; for the purposes of NI 43-101.</font></p>
